# Platform Knowledge: Flink Windowing API Extension Points

## Your Task

Map the extension points in Apache Flink's windowing API that a developer would need to implement a custom window assigner. Find: 1. The abstract base class `WindowAssigner` in `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/` — report its abstract methods. 2. The `MergingWindowAssigner` subclass that adds `mergeWindows()` for session-style windows. 3. The `Trigger` base class in the triggers package — report the lifecycle methods (`onElement`, `onEventTime`, `onProcessingTime`, `onMerge`). 4. An existing reference implementation: `EventTimeSessionWindows` — report how it implements `assignWindows()` and `mergeWindows()`. 5. The `TimeWindow` class that concrete assigners produce. For each, report the file path, class name, and key method signatures.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

Perfect! I've successfully mapped all the extension points in Apache Flink's windowing API. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Findings

I've created `/workspace/answer.json` with comprehensive information about the five core components:

### 1. **WindowAssigner** (Abstract Base Class)
- Location: `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/WindowAssigner.java`
- Abstract methods to implement:
  - `assignWindows()` - assigns windows to elements
  - `getDefaultTrigger()` - provides default trigger
  - `getWindowSerializer()` - handles serialization
  - `isEventTime()` - indicates time mode

### 2. **MergingWindowAssigner** (Subclass for Session-style Windows)
- Location: `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/MergingWindowAssigner.java`
- Key method: `mergeWindows()` - determines which windows should be merged

### 3. **Trigger** (Lifecycle Management)
- Location: `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/Trigger.java`
- Lifecycle methods:
  - `onElement()` - fired when element arrives
  - `onEventTime()` - fired on event-time timers
  - `onProcessingTime()` - fired on processing-time timers
  - `onMerge()` - called when windows merge
  - `clear()` - cleans up window state

### 4. **EventTimeSessionWindows** (Reference Implementation)
- Location: `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/EventTimeSessionWindows.java`
- Creates single window per element spanning `[timestamp, timestamp + sessionTimeout)`
- Delegates merging to `TimeWindow.mergeWindows()`

### 5. **TimeWindow** (Window Type)
- Location: `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/windows/TimeWindow.java`
- Constructor:
